       $(function(){

     $('#vod_widget .programs_list .inner').slimScroll({
        //height: '250px'
         position: 'left',
         color: '#fff',
    });
	
	$('#vod_widget .menu a[data-type!=""].active').click();
	

	var player = $('#vod_widget video').mediaelementplayer({
	    videoWidth: '100%',
	    videoHeight: '370',

		features: ['playpause','current','progress','duration','volume','fullscreen','vast'],
		
		success: function(mediaElement, domObject)
		{
			var one_time = false;
			$(window).on('scroll', function(){
				
				if (one_time) return;
				
				var elem = $('#vod_widget');
				
				var docViewTop = $(window).scrollTop();

				var elemTop = $(elem).offset().top;

				if (elemTop >= docViewTop)
				{
					one_time = true;
					mediaElement.setMuted(true);
					mediaElement.play();
				}
			})
	
		}
		
		//adsPrerollMediaUrl: ['https://video.htv.co.il/2018/Promo/Yarid.mp4 '],
		//adsPrerollAdUrl: ['https://www.payngo.co.il/'],
		//adsPrerollAdEnableSkip: true,
		//adsPrerollAdSkipSeconds: -1
	});
	
    $('#vod_widget .lecturers_slider .owl-carousel').owlCarousel({
	   
        nav: true,
        navText: ['<i class="material-icons dp48">keyboard_arrow_right</i>','<i class="material-icons dp48">keyboard_arrow_left</i>'],
        autoplay: true,
        autoplayTimeout: 3000,
        autoplayHoverPause: true,
        smartSpeed: 500,
        margin: 2,
        loop: true,
		rtl: true,
        autoWidth:true
		
	}); 
    
});
